 treadmill par daud lagaana cardio eksrasij kaa sabase badhiya jariya he
 Losing weight through a trade mill is not as difficult as compared to other machines
 lekin is dauraan kuch saavdhaaniyaan baratani bhi bahut jaruri he
 1
 nange paanv treadmill par naa daudenfriction or tej movement ke chalate kaaphi hit paidaa hoti he
 Therefore, if you run at the trade mill without shoes, your feet may get jealous
 belt ke kinaaron par paanv galati se phisal gaya to gambhir chot bhi aa sakati he
 Apart from this, there is also a risk of fungus and bacteria
 isliye fitting juute pahanakar hi treadmill par daud lagaana chahie
 2
 mashin start karne se pehle belt nahin deck par rakhen paanvvaise to jab bhi aap trade mil ko start karenge, uski shuruaati speed kam hi rahati he
 That is, it does not matter what its speed was during the last time it was closed
 mashin main yah feechar isliye diya jaataa he taaki achaanak tej speed main belt ke ghoomane se aapkaa balance naa bighad jaae
 However, if there is a disturbance in the machine, and the starting speed is more than your capacity, then it is always advisable to spread both your legs on the deck before you turn on the machine
 phir belt kii speed apane hisaab se set karne ke baad hi usapar apana paanv rakhen
 3
 treadmill par daudte vakt kabhi neeche naa dekhexsar aisa hota he ki log thakkar yaa excitement main chalati treadmill par apane pairon ke movement ko nihaarne lagate hai
 But doing so is dangerous because during this time you can lose balance and fall victim to an accident
 isliye daudte vakt hameshaa saamne kii ore dekhen
 In such a situation, you will not have trouble breathing and leaving
 4
 Do not hold the handrail while running It is often the case that people running on the treadmill grab the handrail
 lekin agar aapane aisa lambey samay tak kiya to baanh main akadan hogi or dard shuru ho jayega
 Keep in mind, if you happen to have to resort to handrail in the middle of the size, it means that the speed of your treadmill is more than necessary
 5
 Increase slowly Do not increase the speed of the speedtread mill
 dhire dhire isaki speed badhaane se aapaki body ko varrup kaa bhi samay milegaa or aapaki manshapeshiyon main akadan bhi nahin hogi
 6
 jarurat se zyada naa rakhen trade mil kii speedtreadmill par running se pehle apni 'target heart rate' jaan lijie
 Do not keep too much speed in the cycle of weight loss
 kisi ko bhi apni 'target heart rate' kii 50-70 fisadi speed se zyada par nahin daudna chahie
 If you did not do this, you may have a heart attack
 7
 Never try to get off the running treadmill, even if an urgent call comes or someone is knocking at the door constantly, never get off the moving tread mill
 agar bahut jaruri ho to immergency batan dabaaen, belt jab puri tarah ruk jaae tabhi us par se utren
 Because you can get dizzy when you get off the moving treadmill or you can fall and lose balance
